DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  # Fundamental system updates and core tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      bison \
      flex \
      pkg-config \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      valgrind \
      clang \
      gcc-11 \
      libonig-dev
  # Install jq from source
  WORKDIR /tmp/jq
  RUN wget https://github.com/jqlang/jq/releases/download/jq-1.8.1/jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      cd jq-1.8.1 && \
      ./configure && \
      make && \
      make install
  # Python environment setup
  RUN pip3 install pipenv virtualenv
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/jqlang_jq
  # Copy project files
  COPY . .
  # Cleanup and finalize
  RUN rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* /tmp/*
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  # Fundamental system updates and core tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      bison \
      flex \
      pkg-config \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-venv \
      valgrind \
      clang \
      gcc-11 \
      libonig-dev
  # Install jq from source
  WORKDIR /tmp/jq
  RUN wget https://github.com/jqlang/jq/releases/download/jq-1.8.1/jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      cd jq-1.8.1 && \
      ./configure && \
      make && \
      make install
  # Python environment setup
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir pipenv virtualenv
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /jqlang_jq
  # Copy project files
  COPY . .
  # Configure and build project
  RUN ./configure && make
  # Cleanup and finalize
  RUN rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* /tmp/*
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  # Fundamental system updates and core tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      bison \
      flex \
      pkg-config \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-venv \
      python3-dev \
      valgrind \
      clang \
      gcc-11 \
      libonig-dev
  # Install jq from source
  WORKDIR /tmp/jq
  RUN wget https://github.com/jqlang/jq/releases/download/jq-1.8.1/jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      cd jq-1.8.1 && \
      ./configure && \
      make && \
      make install
  # Python environment setup with explicit pip3 and verbose output
  RUN pip3 install --upgrade pip && \
      pip3 install --verbose --no-cache-dir pipenv virtualenv
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /jqlang_jq
  # Copy project files
  COPY . .
  # Configure and build project
  RUN ./configure && make
  # Cleanup and finalize
  RUN rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* /tmp/*
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 3 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  # Fundamental system updates and core tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      bison \
      flex \
      pkg-config \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-venv \
      python3-dev \
      valgrind \
      clang \
      gcc-11 \
      libonig-dev
  # Install jq from source
  WORKDIR /tmp/jq
  RUN wget https://github.com/jqlang/jq/releases/download/jq-1.8.1/jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      cd jq-1.8.1 && \
      ./configure && \
      make && \
      make install
  # Python environment setup with detailed error handling
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip && \
      python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir setuptools wheel && \
      python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir pipenv virtualenv || \
      (echo "Python package installation detailed error:" && \
       python3 -m pip list && \
       python3 --version && \
       pip3 --version && \
       exit 1)
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /jqlang_jq
  # Copy project files
  COPY . .
  # Configure and build project
  RUN ./configure && make
  # Cleanup and finalize
  RUN rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* /tmp/*
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM debian:12-slim AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  # Fundamental system updates and core tools
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get upgrade -y && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      bison \
      flex \
      pkg-config \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-venv \
      python3-dev \
      valgrind \
      clang \
      gcc-11 \
      libonig-dev
  # Install jq from source
  WORKDIR /tmp/jq
  RUN wget https://github.com/jqlang/jq/releases/download/jq-1.8.1/jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf jq-1.8.1.tar.gz && \
      cd jq-1.8.1 && \
      ./configure && \
      make && \
      make install
  # Python environment setup with improved error handling
  RUN python3 -m pip install --break-system-packages --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python3 -m pip install --break-system-packages pipenv virtualenv
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /jqlang_jq
  # Copy project files
  COPY . .
  # Prepare build environment
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure && \
      make
  # Cleanup and finalize
  RUN rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* /tmp/*
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
